<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="lv"><a href = vnd.unilang:dome.html>dome</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>5th <a href = vnd.unilang:declension.html>declension</a></i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:often.html>often</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plural.html>plural</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:council.html>council</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:legislative.html>legislative</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:administrative.html>administrative</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:organ.html>organ</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="lv">pilsētas <b><a href = vnd.unilang:dome.html>dome</a></b>, <b>domes</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:city.html>city</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:council.html>council</a></b></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="lv"><b>domes</b> vēlēšanas</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:city.html>city</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:council.html>council</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:election.html>elections</a></span></div></dd>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:verb.html>Verb</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
